during hiv therapy there may be an increase in weight and in levels of blood lipids and bleeding . this is partly linked to restored health and life style , and in the case of blood lipids sometimes to the medicines themselves . your doctor will test for these changes . like all medicines , this medicines can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the hospital staff will monitor your condition closely during treatment . tell them immediately if you notice any of the following serious side effects : severe and persistent pain in the abdomen ( stomach area ) which might reach through to your bleeding , as well as bleeding in the brain or bowel . this may be a sign of a serious condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . serious side effects tell your doctor immediately if you notice any of the following : low blood pressure , tiredness , paleness , dizziness , headache , and loss of consciousness . these may be signs of a condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . if you notice any of these signs , seek medical advice immediately . a condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . if you have a combination of any of the following symptoms : test your blood sugar level , test your urine for ketones if you can , then seek medical advice immediately . these may be signs of a very serious condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . most of the side effects are mild to moderate . however , some may be serious and require treatment . serious side effects tell your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following serious side effects : skin rash , which may form blisters and looks like small targets ( central dark spots surrounded by a paler area , with a dark ring around the edge ) ( erythema multiforme ), a widespread rash with blisters and blistering skin , particularly around the mouth , nose , eyes and genitals ( stevens johnson syndrome ), and a more severe form causing skin peeling in more than 2 % of the body surface ( toxic epidermal necrolysis ) signs of serious mental changes or if you notice any of these symptoms , please seek medical advice immediately . these may be signs of a very serious condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . in general , the observed side effects are mild to moderate and will generally disappear after a short time . tell your doctor about any of the following serious side effects straight away : common ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) - a decrease in the number of red blood cells ( anaemia ) - sore throat or cough - high blood pressure ( hypertension ) - chest pain - neck ( abdominal ) pain - feeling sick ( vomiting ) - diarrhoea - loss of appetite ( these may be signs of a condition known as posterior reversible encephalopathy syndrome "). the frequency of this side effect is rare ( may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people ) - blood clots in the veins ( an uncommon side effect that may affect up to 1 in 100 people ) especially in the legs ( symptoms include swelling , pain , and redness in the leg ), which may travel through blood vessels to the lungs causing chest pain and difficulty in breathing . if you notice any of these symptoms seek medical advice immediately ; like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . contact your doctor immediately if you experience : - fever , signs of infection or extreme tiredness . these may be due to rare decrease of some blood cells . - signs of liver problems such as yellowing of the skin and / or the eyes ( jaundice ), whether or not associated with bleeding which appears under the skin as red pinpoint dots and / or confusion ( see section 2 ' take special care with clopidogrel_mylan '). - swelling in the mouth or eyes ( angioedema ) and / or confusion ( see section 2 ' take special care with clopidogrel_mylan '). - swelling in the mouth or eyes ( angioedema ) and / or confusion ( see section 2 ' warnings and precautions '). - swelling in the mouth or head , blood in the urine . in a small number of cases , bleeding in the eye , inside the head , the lung or the joints has also been reported . if you experience prolonged bleeding when taking clopidogrel_mylan . if you cut or injure yourself , it may take longer than usual for bleeding to stop . this is linked to the way your medicine works as it prevents the ability of blood clots to form . for minor cuts and injuries e . g ., cutting yourself , shaving , this is usually of no concern . however , if you are concerned by your bleeding , you should contact your doctor straightaway ( see section 2 ' warnings and precautions '). other side effects include : common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) - diarrhoea , abdominal pain , indigestion or heartburn . - uncommon side effects : headache , stomach ulcer , vomiting , nausea , constipation , excessive gas in stomach or intestines , rashes , itching , dizziness , sensation of tingling and numbness . - rare side effect ( may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people ): - jaundice ; like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the side effects caused by viagra are usually mild to moderate and of a short duration . if you experience any of these , stop using this medicine and contact your doctor straight away . contact your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following : - sudden severe allergic reaction ( e . g . swelling of the face , lips , tongue and / or throat ) - difficulty in breathing or swallowing - sudden drop in blood pressure ; - this occurs rarely ( may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people ). - if you experience a severe allergic reaction , stop taking viagra and see a doctor straight away , if you notice any of the following serious side effects : - severe and persistent pain in the abdomen ( stomach area ) which might reach through to your eyes , as well as fever and seizures , as it could be a sign of an inflamed pancreas ( inflamed pancreas ). - if you experience a combination of any of the following symptoms : - swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat and difficulty breathing . contact your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following : - seizures , seizures or stroke ( seeing or hearing things that are not there ) - difficulty in breathing and / or throat swelling of the face , lips , tongue and / or throat that may cause difficulty in breathing or swallowing , stop taking this medicine and call your doctor straight away . your doctor may prescribe a medicine to treat your allergic reaction and a different medicine for your diabetes . rare ( may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people ) if you have a serious allergic reaction , including : - swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat and difficulty breathing . contact your doctor immediately if you experience any of the following symptoms : - swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue and / or throat and difficulty in breathing . - if you notice any of these symptoms seek medical advice immediately ; - a severe allergic reaction ( e . g . swelling of the face , lips , tongue and / or throat ) - fever and / or seizures ( see section " warnings and precautions '). - swelling in the mouth or throat . - if you notice any of these symptoms , contact your doctor as soon as possible . the other side effects that have been experienced by some patients when viagra is taken with other antidiabetic medicines are : - like all medicines , zerene can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some of these side effects may be serious and need immediate medical attention . the frequency of these side effects is not known ( cannot be estimated from the available data ). if you notice any of the following serious side effects , stop taking zerene and see a doctor straight away . the frequency of the side effects listed below is defined using the following convention : very common side effects ( may affect more than double_vision in 10 people ) side effects are : common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 36 people ) dizziness , decreased appetite , apathy , restlessness , agitation , irritability , nightmares , nightmares , balance disorder ( see also " warnings and precautions " earlier in section section 2 ). tell your doctor if you experience any of these side effects . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in extremities appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
